The description provided suggests traits that might not necessarily correlate directly with the ability to do a "thorough job." High extraversion and openness can indicate a person who is energetic and imaginative, but they do not inherently guarantee attention to detail or thoroughness in work. Thus, while these traits might contribute to various aspects of life and work, they don't specifically align with the notion of doing a thorough job.
